    <!-- WP Dark Mode – No FOUC Fix -->
    <script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
    (function() {
        function getCookie(name) {
            const match = document.cookie.match(new RegExp('(?:^|; )' + name + '=([^;]*)'));
            return match ? decodeURIComponent(match[1]) : null;
        }

        var choice = getCookie('wp-dark-mode-choice');
        var device = getCookie('wp-dark-mode-device');
        var enableDark = choice === 'dark' || (!choice && device === 'dark');

        if (enableDark) document.documentElement.classList.add('wp-dark-mode-active');
    })();
    </script>

<script type="rocketlazyloadscript"> 
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
  const sidebar = document.querySelector('#sidebar');
  const block7 = document.querySelector('#block-7');

  if (sidebar && block7) {
    const sidebarHeight = sidebar.offsetHeight;
    const contentHeight = block7.offsetTop + block7.offsetHeight;
    const paddingNeeded = sidebarHeight - contentHeight;

    if (paddingNeeded > 0) {
      block7.style.marginTop = `${paddingNeeded}px`;
    }
  }
});
</script>

<script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
  const toggleBtn = document.getElementById("socialBtn");
  const modal = document.getElementById("socialModal");
  const closeBtn = document.getElementById("closeSocials");

  toggleBtn.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    modal.classList.toggle("active");
  });

  closeBtn.addEventListener("click", function () {
    modal.classList.remove("active");
  });

  // Optional: close modal when clicking outside
  window.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
    if (!modal.contains(e.target) && !toggleBtn.contains(e.target)) {
      modal.classList.remove("active");
    }
  });
});
</script>
